NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

[Part VI—Sec. 4

PUBLIC NOTICE
I, S. SATHISH a male child born to Loganathan on 26th April 1988 residing at No. 13/A, P.P. Garden 5th Main Street,
2nd Floor, Aminjikarai, Chennai-29, has been living as a Female after an elaborate sexual reassignment surgery by
Dr. Jayaraman, (S.Mech, MNAMs., Dip. N.B., Ph, FICS, Professor of Plastic Surgery, Kilpauk Medical College Hospital,
Chennai-10) By this I, may be treated as a Female and shall henceforth be known as S. SARRAH MARY.
Chennai,
30th November 2016.

S. SATHISH.
